class="MsoNormal">   <span style="color:#fff;"><b><span style="font-size: 14pt; font-family: Arial; ">&nbsp;</span></b></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify">   <span style="color:#fff;"><b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; ">LAS VEGAS (July 18, 2012)</span></b><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; "> &ndash; Due to the filming schedule of the hit NBC television show <i>The Voice</i>, the premiere of &ldquo;CeeLo Green is LOBERACE&rdquo; at Planet Hollywood Resort &amp; Casino has been postponed until 2013.</span></span><span style="font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Arial;mso-bidi-font-family:Arial"><o:p></o:p></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify">   <span style="color:#fff;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; ">&nbsp;</span></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify">   <span style="color:#fff;"><span style="font-size: 10pt; font-family: Arial; ">&ldquo;It&#39;s always been a dream of mine to be among the great music legends who have had a Las Vegas residency and I was very much looking forward to launching &lsquo;Loberace&rsquo; this year,&rdquo; states CeeLo Green. &ldquo;But, as we move into the third season of <i>The Voice</i>, with my dedicated commitment to the filming schedule and love for my role on the show, I will need to postpone the opening of 363	0	CEELO GREEN & SISTER SHEDONNA LAUNCH GREENHOUSE FOUNDATION			<p>   &nbsp;</p>  <p class="p1">   &nbsp;</p>  <p class="p2">   CEELO GREEN &amp; SISTER SHEDONNA LAUNCH GREENHOUSE FOUNDATION</p>  <p class="p2">   <i>Educating and Empowering Our Youth to Live, Love &amp; Be Green</i></p>  <p class="p3">   &nbsp;</p>  <p class="p3">   Atlanta, GA (August 14<span class="s1"><sup>th</sup></span>, 2012) &ndash; In the words of <b>Kermit the Frog</b>, &ldquo;It&rsquo;s not easy being green.&rdquo;&nbsp; But, Grammy Award Winning artist <b>CeeLo Green</b> and his sister <b>Shedonna Alexander</b> have together co-founded the <a href="http://ghfoundation.org/"><span class="s2"><b>GreenHouse Foundation</b></span></a><b>, </b>a non-profit organization with a mission to help make &ldquo;green education&rdquo; easier and accessible to students in underserved school districts. The <b>GreenHouse Foundation</b> will educate, inspire and influence children to become responsible stewards of their environment, communities and future.</p>  <p class="p4">   &nbsp;</p>  <p class="p3">   Officially launching on <b>August 17</b><span class="s1"><b><sup>th</sup></b></span><b> </b>in <b>Atlanta, GA</b>, this sibling team will dedicate their first &ldquo;teaching GreenHouse&rdquo; in memory of their late mother <b>Sheila J. Callaway Tyler</b>. The dedication will take place on the campus of <b>Southwest Atlanta Christian Academy</b>, a &ldquo;GreenHouse School Partner&rdquo;, where CeeLo attended elementary school. <i>(Please see Media Alert below for more details.)</i></p>  <p class="p3">   &nbsp;</p>  <p class="p3">   The GreenHouse Foundation is an extension of CeeLo and Shedonna&rsquo;s long family<b> </b>legacy of philanthropy. They grew up surrounded by great role models &ndash; their maternal grandmother <b>Ruby Callaway Robinson </b>and mother<b> Sheila J. Callaway Tyler.</b>&nbsp; Ruby started a nationally recognized non-profit organization &ldquo;<b>Comprehensive Auxiliary for Southwest Community on Alcohol and Drug Education</b>&rdquo; (CASCADE) that focused on drug-prevention and education in underprivileged communities. She initiated the nationwide &ldquo;<b>Just Say No</b>&rdquo; kids march in May 1986, which drew over five million participants and achieved broad and tremendous support, including recognition from former <b>First Lady Nancy Reagan</b> and <b>Soliel Moon Fry </b>aka &ldquo;<b>Punkie Brewster&rdquo;</b>. Their late mother <b>Sheila </b>followed in her mother&rsquo;s footsteps, serving as one of the first female firefighters with the Atlanta Fire Department, plus years of other volunteer work throughout the community.</p>  <p class="p3">   <b>&nbsp;</b></p>  <p class="p3">   The youth are our future leaders, so CeeLo and Shedonna recognize the importance of empowering children to love and protect the planet. As a result, the GreenHouse Foundation&rsquo;s first initiative is the &ldquo;Green Garden Education Program,&rdquo; which will offer schools an opportunity to become &quot;GreenHouse School Partners&rdquo; and start making their green footprint. Through this program, the GreenHouse Foundation will build outdoor green gardens on campuses and introduce &ldquo;green education&rdquo; into their everyday curriculum, teaching children the importance of &ldquo;being green&rdquo;.</p>  <p class="p3">   &nbsp;</p>  <p class="p3">   &ldquo;The Green Garden program will use outdoor gardening as an innovative tool to teach math and science. It will allow students to experience a new approach to &ldquo;green education,&rdquo; states co-founder <b>Shedonna Alexander</b>. &ldquo;We are committed to the mission to empower children with the knowledge, attitude and desire to positively influence their futures, their communities and the long-term sustainability of their planet.&rdquo;</p>  <p class="p3">   &nbsp;</p>  <p class="p3">   The <b>University of Georgia</b>&rsquo;s Cooperative Extension service for Atlanta&rsquo;s Fulton County is playing a key role in the GreenHouse Foundation&rsquo;s education and community outreach.&nbsp; UGA Cooperative Extension extends lifelong learning to the people of Georgia through unbiased, research-based education in agriculture, the environment, communities, youth and families. As part of the GreenHouse School Partnership and Green Garden Education Program, they are providing curriculum support through their agricultural and family sciences programs.</p>  <p class="p3">   &nbsp;</p>  <p class="p3">   &ldquo;Through the Green Garden Education Program, the GreenHouse Foundation is supporting schools with the tools, curriculum, and resources necessary to create and maintain an outdoor &lsquo;teaching garden&rsquo;. With the garden as the primary focus, children will learn the fundamentals of gardening along with the health and environmental benefits of growing their own produce. Children will also learn how to start and manage their own school farmers market,&rdquo; explains co-founder <b>CeeLo Green</b>. &ldquo;The hands of our children will help feed those in need, like the homeless or elderly who live in &lsquo;grocery deserts&rsquo; with no access to fresh produce.&rdquo;</p>  <p class="p3">   &nbsp;</p>  <p class="p3">   In the future, the GreenHouse Foundation plans to launch other initiatives such as &ldquo;<i>The School Waste Diversion Initiative</i>&rdquo;, which will provide schools with waste receptacles to divert non-biodegradable waste from local landfills and create a local competition among the schools. Annually on Earth Day, they will start &ldquo;<i>The Clean Atlanta Green Day</i>&rdquo; to unify the city&rsquo;s local businesses, schools and government officials to collectively clean up the City of Atlanta. Another key initiative will be the launch of &ldquo;<i>The GreenHouse Community Gardens Program</i>&rdquo;, which will take the concept of their on-campus &ldquo;school gardens&rdquo; to the next level by adopting land around Atlanta to develop organic community gardens maintained by volunteers. Additionally, the GreenHouse Foundation will also create a &ldquo;<i>Green Collar Career Development &amp; Training Program</i>&rdquo; that will introduce and educate students on jobs that impact our environment. As the foundation grows larger, it will also offer students the opportunity to earn the &ldquo;<i>Green Career College Scholarship</i>&rdquo; based on academic performance. <b>Teach Green, See Green, Live Green &ndash; GreenHouse Foundation.</b></p>  <p class="p3">   <b>&nbsp;</b></p>  <p class="p2">   <b>GET SOCIAL WITH GREENHOUSE FOUNDATION</b></p>  <p class="p2">   <b>Official Website</b>: <a href="http://www.ghfoundation.org/">www.GHFoundation.org</a></p>  <p class="p2">   <b>Twitter:&nbsp; </b>@GreenHouseFound / <a href="http://bit.ly/Rmp1kD">http://bit.ly/Rmp1kD</a></p>  <p class="p5">   <span class="s3"><b>Facebook: </b><a href="http://on.fb.me/RulNf0"><span class="s4">http://on.fb.me/RulNf0</span></a></span></p>  <p class="p6">   <b>&nbsp;</b></p>	2012-08-14 21:54:00.000	2012-08-14 21:54:00.000	2022-08-14 00:00:00.000	1	Ceelo Green Greenhouse Foundation Charity Launch	http://www.ceelogreen.com/news,view_363.htm

season, fans will take center stage in the primetime television pageantry, joined by Grammy Award-winning artist <b>CeeLo Green</b> who will sing NFL Network&rsquo;s new <i>Thursday Night Football&nbsp;</i></span><span style="font-size: 11pt; ">anthem with the fans.&nbsp;</span></span></p>  <p class="MsoNormal">  <!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--> <span style="color:#fff;"><span football,&rdquo; CeeLo said. &ldquo;The NFL always brings us the biggest and brightest entertainment spectacle in sports and now with &lsquo;Fanchise,&rsquo; NFL Network gives loyal fans the chance to participate! ">Each&nbsp;<i>Thursday Night Football</i>&nbsp;game will feature fan videos specific to that night&rsquo;s matchup, starting with Chicago Bears and Green Bay Packers fans singing the chorus along with CeeLo for the first <i>TNF</i> game on September 13 (Chicago at Green Bay, 8:00 PM ET).<br />   <!--[if !supportLineBreakNewLine]--><br />   </span></span><!--[endif]--><o:p></o:p></p>  <p class="MsoNormal" style="text-align:justify">   <span style="color:#fff;"><span style="font-size: 11pt; CeeLo's 1st-ever autobiography, "Everybody's Brother," out 9/10/13	<p style="text-align: center;">   FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE<br />   <br />   EVERYBODY&rsquo;S BROTHER: My Story<br />   By CeeLo Green<br />   With Big Gipp and David Wild<br />   Grand Central Publishing<br />   Publication date: September 10, 2013<br />   $28.00 | Hardcover | ISBN: 978-1455516674</p>  <p style="text-align: center;">   <br />   <span style="font-size:14px;"><br />   EVERYBODY&rsquo;S BROTHER<br />   My Story<br />   By CeeLo Green</span></p>  <p style="text-align: center;">   <img alt="" height="855" src="/ugc-1/1/1/0/everybodysbrother_finalcover_withgra.jpg" width="560" /><br />   <br />   CeeLo (who seems to be moving toward single-name status) is a funny guy with a colorful story to share&hellip; [EVERYBODY&rsquo;S BROTHER is] an &lsquo;only in America&rsquo; story with Horatio Alger as a rapper and neo-soul singer.&rdquo;<br />   &mdash;Kirkus Reviews<br />   <br />   &ldquo;Brassy, often snarky, and totally madcap, Cee Lo mouths off in this ribald tell-all, to the enjoyment of his fans and newbies everywhere.&rdquo;<br />   &mdash;Publishers Weekly<br />   <br />   <br />   CeeLo Green dresses as Liberace, performs with the Muppets, and does 360-degree flips with a grand piano at his fingertips. He&#39;s a coach on the #1-rated network reality show, The Voice, and is a genre-breaking artist who has garnered millions of fans over his music career releasing albums as Goodie Mob, Gnarls Barkley and of course as CeeLo Green himself. He has largely remained a man of Mystery&hellip;until now. <br />   <br />   CeeLo Green has penned his first memoir, or as he refers to it, a &ldquo;psychedelic fable,&rdquo; entitled EVERYBODY&rsquo;S BROTHER: My Story by CeeLo Green with Big Gipp and David Wild [Grand Central Publishing | $28.00 | Hardcover], which is being released on September 10th, 2013. In the memoir, the Grammy Award winner finally reveals his remarkable personal story including tales from his childhood, his search to find his voice and how he maintained his individuality while rising to the top. At times gritty, yet always truthful, EVERYBODY&rsquo;S BROTHER illustrates how CeeLo Green created the artist who he is today, despite circumstances beyond his control. Threaded through with hope, inspiration, and real advice, along with anecdotes and revealing insights from CeeLo&#39;s childhood friend, Goodie Mob band-member and &quot;brother from another mother&quot; Big Gipp, EVERYBODY&rsquo;S BROTHER shows how CeeLo found the power in his own voice, and defied the odds time and time again. Filled with exclusive pictures from CeeLo&rsquo;s childhood, plus images documenting each stage in his life and career, this new memoir truly tells the real story of CeeLo Green from day one to today. Both in his tone and in his look, EVERYBODY&#39;S BROTHER is a theatrical and inspiring artistic statement that perfectly captures its memorable, maverick author. <br />   <br />   As CeeLo writes in the book&rsquo;s introduction:</p>  <p style="text-align: center;">   &ldquo;I write this book not just to celebrate my own voice and to revel in my own success story, but to help encourage the next generation of underdogs to listen closely to the voices in their own heads, so that maybe someday they can rise up and share their own voices with the world too.&rdquo;<br />   <br />   <br />   <br />   ABOUT THE AUTHOR<br />   <br />   A member of the Goodie Mob and the front-member to Gnarls Barkley (winner of two 2007 Grammys and known for their #1 hit &quot;Crazy&quot;), CeeLo Green was born in Atlanta and helped turn the city into the center of a major hip-hop/rap revolution. He is a multi-award winning musician, as well as one of the celebrity coaches on NBC&#39;s #1 reality television show The Voice. <br />   <br />   Big Gipp helped CeeLo start his music career when he introduced him to the members of the Goodie Mob when CeeLo was just 17. They have been brothers ever since. In addition to being a member of Goodie Mob, Gipp also has a solo career and has contributed to several collaborations with other artists over the years. <br />   <br />   David Wild is a New York Times bestselling author, a contributing editor to Rolling Stone, and an Emmy-nominated television writer and producer, as well as a popular blogger for Huffington Post and a frequent television commentator about popular music. He lives in Los Angeles with his wife and two sons.<br />   <br />   Also available in downloadable and e-book (978-1455516681) formats.<br />   <span style="font-size:14px;">Pre-order your copy below<br />   <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Everybodys-Brother-CeeLo-Green/dp/1455516678" target="_blank">AMAZON<br />   i</a><a href="https://itunes.apple.com/us/book/everybodys-brother/id599705105?mt=11" target="_blank">Tunes<br />   B</a><a href="http://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/everybodys-brother-green-ceelo/1115837450?ean=9781455581405" target="_blank">arnes &amp; Noble<br />   I</a><a href="http://www.indiebound.org/book/9781455516674" target="_blank">ndie Bound</a></span></p>  	2013-09-03 17:05:00.000	2013-09-03 17:05:00.000	2023-09-03 00:00:00.000	1	ceelo,book,autobiography,cee lo,cee lo,everybodys brother,everybody's brother	http://www.ceelogreen.com/news,view_449.htm
